<strong>Classification:</strong> M<br/>

<strong>Country:</strong> United States<br/>
<br/>
<strong>Release date:</strong> 26/01/2011<br/>
<strong>Release details:</strong> Limited national release. Check newspapers for screening dates or contact the distributor for further details.<br/>
<strong>Genre:</strong> Adventure, Drama, Western<br/>
<strong>Lead actor:</strong> Jeff Bridges<br/>

<p class="description">A tough U.S. Marshal helps a stubborn young woman track down her father's murderer.</p>
<p class="score"> Margaret: <img alt="four stars" class="rating" src="/web/20141229143225im_/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/img/stars-four.png"/> David: <img alt="four-and-a-half stars" class="rating" src="/web/20141229143225im_/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/img/stars-four-and-a-half.png"/> </p>

<div id="theReview">
<h2>True Grit</h2>
<p class="ratd"> Rated <em>M</em></p>
<p>Margaret and David have a general discussion about some movies which opened over the Christmas/New Year Period.</p>
<h2>Further comments</h2>
<p>MARGARET: David, I know you're a major fan of TRUE GRIT.<br/><br/>DAVID: Yes, the new version of TRUE GRIT. I like the old one too, which was made in 1969 which won John Wayne an Oscar and which was really one of the last in a great series of sort of classical westerns in which John Wayne had starred. The western film would be turned upside-down a few months after its release when THE WILD BUNCH opened.<br/><br/>MARGARET: Yes.<br/><br/>DAVID: So that was very different, I think, an approach from this. They are both based on the same book by Charles Portis but the Coen brothers, in the new TRUE GRIT, really went back to the source and they created at film with a different sort of mood; a much darker mood, I think.<br/><br/>MARGARET: Do you know, I bothered to look at the old one again and they are so similar, the two films. <br/><br/>DAVID: I don't agree at all. I bothered to look at it too, but I don't think they are.<br/><br/>MARGARET: I think the ending is different and I actually prefer the ending in the old one. <br/><br/>DAVID: Really?<br/><br/>MARGARET: Yes, I do.<br/><br/>DAVID: Oh, yes.<br/><br/>MARGARET: It's more sentimental, I know, but it worked for me. But I think both films have a sort of a ruthlessness in them that I thought was really effective and I thought Kim Darby, who plays the young woman in the first film, was amazingly good.<br/><br/>DAVID: She was good but not as good as Hailee Steinfeld, who plays her in the new one, who is much closer to the real age. I think she was 13 years old when she did the film.<br/><br/>MARGARET: Well, I don't know. I thought they were both pretty good.<br/><br/>DAVID: I love the look of the new one. Roger Deakin's photography is so wonderful.<br/><br/>MARGARET: Look, it looks fantastic but it was like seeing the same film over again, I have to tell you.<br/><br/>DAVID: I don't find them the same at all. Did you like the use of the music - that hymn that they use?<br/><br/>MARGARET: Yes.<br/><br/>DAVID: Which is the hymn that Charles Laughton uses in THE NIGHT OF THE HUNTER.<br/><br/>MARGARET: I know, but it's also... they're using Carter Burwell's music again. <br/><br/>DAVID: Yes.<br/><br/>MARGARET: You know, he's done just about every film, I think, of theirs and I love his music. I think it's terrific. I know that Jeff Bridges is accused of being unintelligible and I think the problem with the film is that if you can't understand what he says, then you miss so much of the humour in the film because it's the way he says stuff, the way he expresses himself that is...<br/><br/>DAVID: Well, all the dialogue is beautiful, I think. <br/><br/>MARGARET: But it's funny. He's funny. It's gorgeous. I really, really enjoyed it. I think it's a really super film.</p>

<h3>Charles :</h3>
<p class="date">16 Jun 2013 6:13:28pm</p>
<p class="comment">((True Grit))[[10]]<br>Sometimes, great films reach the pinochle of combined art. They capture all their embedded art forms in harmonious syntactical unison . Writing, music, acting, directing, photography, all wonderfully entwined to create a true masterpiece of combined geniuses. In those rare moments of wonderful coexistence of such variant diverse but synergistic art forms, you stand in awe of what makes this specific art form so truly uniquely special. Cohen brothers, I bow before you and your fellow craftsman and women.  A masterpiece before me I have witnessed.</br></p>

<a id="m_ucMessageDisplay13087_m_anchMessageAnchor" name="m13087"></a>
<h3>littlemurders :</h3>
<p class="date">16 Feb 2012 1:35:26pm</p>
<p class="comment">((True Grit))[[7]]<br>As a Cohen Bros fan, I was hoping to give this five stars, having high expectations of  dialogue tinged with irony and wit.  Unfortunately, I couldn't discern the mutterings of its protagonist, Rooster Cogburn.  I didn't have that problem with John Wayne in the original.  Just as well, as I had to rely on my memory from the 1969 film to glean what was happening in this one thanks to the mumbling Starman.  I was also hoping for a Fargo feel, rather than just a slick re-hash. Nonetheless, I enjoyed the landscape, the gritty girl and the chase.</br></p>
<p class="links">
<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20141229143225/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/AlertModerator.aspx?b=117&amp;m=13087&amp;tpa=&amp;r=%2ftmb%2fView%2fMessage.aspx%3fb%3d117%26t%3d198%26a%3d0%26ps%3d50%26tpa%3d%26uto%3d1%26dm%3d4%26ci%3d0%26pd%3d1%26so%3dDateTime%26soa%3dFalse%26p%3d1%26p2%3d0" onclick="return popup(this.href);">Alert moderator</a>

<h3>John :</h3>
<p class="date">09 Aug 2011 4:18:54pm</p>
<p class="comment">((True Grit))[[7]]<br>I have to admit than when I walked into this film I wasent expecting much. Westerns have never been a genre that interested me much, due mostly to stories and characters that felt dull and boring. This film helped get Westerns back onto my tasting plate. While I found the story still lacking in the interest department the characters and the performances by all the actors, most notably Jeff Bridges and Matt Damen were outstanding. The dialogue in this film is well thought  out and with plently of humour  to keep it entertaining all the way to the end.</br></p>
<p class="links">

<a id="m_ucMessageDisplay8555_m_anchMessageAnchor" name="m8555"></a>
<h3>Waz :</h3>
<p class="date">13 Jul 2011 4:25:19pm</p>
<p class="comment">((True Grit))[[8]]<br>A thought that the modern Western was a dying genre, I hadn't seen one in years, that was actually a decent attempt. The Coen Brothers are excellent directors, and full credit to them, like with FARGO and NO COUNTRY FOR OLD MEN, they delivered. Occasionally I found it hard to understand what Bridges was saying sometimes, but full credit to him, and the rest of the cast, they performed brilliantly. This movie has restored faith in the western genre, and is the best one I've seen in a long time. Great filmmaking is what you expect from the Coen Brothers...</br></p>
<p class="links">
<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20141229143225/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/AlertModerator.aspx?b=117&amp;m=8555&amp;tpa=&amp;r=%2ftmb%2fView%2fMessage.aspx%3fb%3d117%26t%3d198%26a%3d0%26ps%3d50%26tpa%3d%26uto%3d1%26dm%3d4%26ci%3d0%26pd%3d1%26so%3dDateTime%26soa%3dFalse%26p%3d1%26p2%3d0" onclick="return popup(this.href);">Alert moderator</a>

<p class="comment">((True Grit))[[8]]<br>This was indeed a gritty, blood-soaked old-fashioned western of the kind which is unknown today. 		$("#mobileMenu").slideToggle('fast');
		$("#btnMobileMenu").toggleClass("buttonOn");
		dcsMultiTrack('DCS.dcsuri', 'ATM Mobile Menu Button', 'WT.ti', 'At the Movies Nav', 'WT.dl', '99');

	$("#finda").focus(function() {
		$("body").scrollTo('#finda',1000);
		return false;
	});		
	
	$('#finda').autocomplete({
		lookup: movies,

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">


var newtopicKey;

$(document).ready(function(){

audShow();
changeAction();
formatComments();

// end ready
});	

function audShow() {
	// display word count only if js enabled
	document.getElementById("wordCount").style.display='inline';
	document.getElementById("audiencecomment").style.display='block';
	if (document.getElementById("allnewComments")) {
		document.getElementById("allnewComments").innerHTML = document.getElementById("loadComments").innerHTML;
	}
}


function changeAction() {
	// avoids non-js form submission 
	var tmpStoryid = "??StoryID??";
	if (document.m_frmMainForm) {
		document.m_frmMainForm.action = 'https://web.archive.org/web/20141229143225/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/NewMessage.aspx?b=117&amp;tn='+tmpStoryid+'&amp;dm=1&amp;tpa=&amp;r=&amp;layout=popup';
		}
}



function formatComments() {
	// replace H3 tag with 'Name:' + name
	var arrayH3 = document.getElementById("comments").getElementsByTagName("h3");
	for (var i = 0; i < arrayH3.length; i++) {
		var theString = arrayH3[i].innerHTML;
		theString = theString.replace(":", "");
		theString = "Name: "+theString;
		arrayH3[i].innerHTML = 	theString;
	}
	// add rating value to each comment
	var arrayComment = getElementsByClassName( 'comment', 'p' );	
	for (var c = 0; c < arrayComment.length; c++) {
		var theComment = arrayComment[c].innerHTML;
		theComment = theComment.replace("[[", "<span class='userRating'>Rating: <img src='https://web.archive.org/web/20141229143225/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/audience/stars").replace("]]",".png' alt='rating'></span>").replace("((", "<!-- ").replace(")))", "))").replace("))", "-->");
		arrayComment[c].innerHTML = theComment;
	}

	
}


function formCheck(zeForm) {
	// pass key to form
	document.getElementById("keyField").value = newtopicKey;
	// basic validation
	if (document.getElementById("yname").value.length < 1) {
		alert("Please enter your name or nickname.");
		document.getElementById("yname").style.background='#FFFDC8';
		return false;
	}
	if (document.getElementById("yemail").value.length < 6) {
		alert("Please enter a valid email address.");
		document.getElementById("yemail").style.background='#FFFDC8';
		return false;
	}
	if (zeForm.score.options[0].selected && zeForm.score.options[0].value=="na") {
		alert("You forgot to rate the movie!");
		document.getElementById("score").style.background='#FFFDC8';	
		return false;
	}	
	// check for http
	spamcheck=zeForm.m_tbxText.value;
	if (spamcheck.indexOf("http")!=-1) {
		document.m_frmMainForm.action = 'https://web.archive.org/web/20141229143225/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/audience/blank.htm';
	}
	// check word count
	wct = cnt(zeForm.m_tbxText.value);
	if (wct > 100) {
		alert("Comments are limited to 100 words. You've written "+wct+" words!");
		document.getElementById("remark").style.background='#FFFDC8';
		return false;	
	}
	
	// replace usual suspect bad characters 
	badChars = Array  ('', '', '', '', '', 'ö', 'é', 'è', 'ñ', 'â', ' ', '','','´');
	goodChars = Array ('...', '-', '-', '"', '"', 'o', 'e', 'e', 'n', 'a', ' ', '\'','\'','\'');
	fld = document.getElementById("remark");
	for(i=0;i<badChars.length;i++){
		restring = new RegExp( badChars[i] , 'g');
		fld.value = fld.value.replace(restring,goodChars[i]);
	}
	fldn = document.getElementById("yname");
	for(j=0;j<badChars.length;j++){
		restringj = new RegExp( badChars[j] , 'g');
		fldn.value = fldn.value.replace(restringj,goodChars[j]);
	}	
	
	// add rating to comment field in [[ ]] tags 
	var theSel = zeForm.score.selectedIndex;
	var theRating = zeForm.score[theSel].value; 
	zeForm.m_tbxText.value = "[["+theRating+"]]\n" + zeForm.m_tbxText.value;
	
	// add movie title to comment field in (( )) tags 
	zeForm.m_tbxText.value = "(("+theMovie+"))" + zeForm.m_tbxText.value;	
	
	// display thankyou div layer and hide form. 
	document.getElementById("favFormThx").style.display='block';
	document.getElementById("favForm").style.display='none';
	document.getElementById("wordCount").style.display='none';	
	
	// all clear, submit the form
	return true;
}

// word count function
function cnt(theform){
	var y=theform;
	var r = 0;
	a=y.replace('\n',' ');
	a=a.split(' ');
	for (z=0; z<a.length; z++) {if (a[z].length > 0) r++;}
	return r;
}

function remainingWords(textAreaContent,textAreaContentValue, maxWords) 
{
	// Determine the number of words we have left
	var numberofwords = cnt(textAreaContentValue);
	wordsLeft = maxWords - numberofwords;
	if (wordsLeft < 1)
	{	// if 100 change color to red
		document.getElementById("wcNum").style.color='red'; 
	} else {
		document.getElementById("wcNum").style.color='#ffffff'; 
	}
	// update word count number
	document.getElementById("wcNum").innerHTML=(0+numberofwords);
}

// windows media alt box
function showWindows() {
	document.getElementById("windowsMed").style.display='block';
}


// generic get by class name
function getElementsByClassName(strClass, strTag, objContElm) {
  strTag = strTag || "*";
  objContElm = objContElm || document;    
  var objColl = objContElm.getElementsByTagName(strTag);
  if (!objColl.length &&  strTag == "*" &&  objContElm.all) objColl = objContElm.all;
  var arr = new Array();                              
  var delim = strClass.indexOf('|') != -1  ? '|' : ' ';   
  var arrClass = strClass.split(delim);    
  for (var i = 0, j = objColl.length; i < j; i++) {                         
    var arrObjClass = objColl[i].className.split(' ');   
    if (delim == ' ' && arrClass.length > arrObjClass.length) continue;
    var c = 0;
    comparisonLoop:
    for (var k = 0, l = arrObjClass.length; k < l; k++) {
      for (var m = 0, n = arrClass.length; m < n; m++) {
        if (arrClass[m] == arrObjClass[k]) c++;
        if ((delim == '|' && c == 1) || (delim == ' ' && c == arrClass.length)) {
          arr.push(objColl[i]); 
          break comparisonLoop;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return arr; 
}

// called from 'new discussion' page in iframe
function sayHello(theKey) {
	newtopicKey = theKey;
}

document.domain = "abc.net.au";
